         <a name=\"content\"></a>\n                    \n                    \n    \n\n\t<article class=\"article-wrapper news\">\n        <div class=\"article-headline\">#Gators Live Blog: #Swamp17 National Signing Day</div>\n        <div class=\"article-subheadline\">Check out our coverage throughout National Signing Day here as the Gators close out the 2017 recruiting class.</div>\n        <div class=\"article-byline\">By Scott Carter, Senior Writer |    Wednesday, February 1, 2017</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t<div class=\"article-image\">\n        <div id=\"ctl00_cplhMainContent_ctl00_story_media_divImage\" class=\"media_object_image\" style=\"width:730px;;\">\n        \n            \n                <img id=\"ctl00_cplhMainContent_ctl00_story_media_imgPrimary\" src=\"/common/controls/image_handler.aspx?thumb_prefix=rp_primary&amp;image_path=/images/2017/1/30/17FB_NSD_Signing17_story_3.jpg\" alt=\"2017 Football - National Signing Day\" style=\"border-width:0px;z-index:1\">\n            \n            \n            <div id=\"ctl00_cplhMainContent_ctl00_story_media_divCaption\" class=\"media_object_caption\" style=\"width:730px;;\"><div class=\"media_object_inner_caption\">National Signing Day has arrived as the Gators seek a strong finish to round out the 2017 class.</div></div>\n            <div style=\"clear:both\"></div>\n            \n        </div>\n         \n    </div>\n\t\t<div class=\"article-content\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"article-links\">\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t <strong>Post: 6:15 p.m.</strong> <em>(Last one to this blog; check out another story on website later)</em><br>\n<br>\nGAINESVILLE, Fla. -- Gators coach <dfn><a href=\"/coaches.aspx?rc=649\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"649\" id=\"sidearmAd1\">Jim McElwain</a></dfn>'s National Signing Day press conference included cheerleaders, the pep band and a few Rowdy Reptiles to welcome him at the door.<br>\n<br>\nIt also included the late addition of &nbsp;receiver <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10346\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10346\" id=\"sidearmAd2\">James Robinson</a></dfn> from Lakeland High. Robinson and running back <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10347\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10347\" id=\"sidearmAd3\">Adarius Lemons</a></dfn> out of Clearwater High added some pop to the Gators' 2017 class as the last two players to officially sign on Wednesday.<br>\n<br>\nRobinson is a 6-foot-4, 205-pound target that played at the same high school that has produced many notable Gators over the years, including the Pouncey brothers, Ahmad Black and Chris Rainey.<br>\n<br>\nLemons rushed for more than 2,000 yards in his prep career and 27 touchdowns, joining Tampa Jesuit product <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10336\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10336\" id=\"sidearmAd4\">Malik Davis</a></dfn> as the running backs in this class.<br>\n<br>\n\"I can't tell you how excited I am for the day, how excited we are as a program,'' McElwain said. \"Things are trending so fastly upward I can't believe it.\"<br>\n<br>\nPrior to McElwain's press conference, Gators defensive line coach <dfn><a href=\"/coaches.aspx?rc=653\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"653\" id=\"sidearmAd5\">Chris Rumph</a></dfn> spent a few minutes discussing the newest members of his position group: T.J. Slaton, <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10338\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10338\" id=\"sidearmAd6\">Zachary Carter</a></dfn>, Elijah Confliffe and early enrollee <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10321\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10321\" id=\"sidearmAd7\">Kyree Campbell</a></dfn>.<br>\n<br>\nCheck out what Rumph had to say in the video below:<br>\n<br>\n<iframe align=\"\" allowfullscreen=\"\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"360\" src=\"/showcase/embed.aspx?Archive=5277&amp;autoplay=false\" width=\"640\"></iframe><br>\n<br>\n<br>\n<strong>Post 2:30 p.m.</strong><br>\n<br>\nGAINESVILLE, Fla. -- The Gators added their 16th signee this afternoon when defensive back <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10345\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10345\" id=\"sidearmAd8\">Brian Edwards</a></dfn> (6-3, 195) out of Miramar High in South Florida made it official.<br>\n<br>\nEdwards is the sixth defensive back to sign today and provides UF with some serious depth at the position heading into the 2017 season. Florida head coach <dfn><a href=\"/coaches.aspx?rc=649\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"649\" id=\"sidearmAd9\">Jim McElwain</a></dfn> is schedule to hold a press conference at around 3:15 in the team's indoor practice facility.<br>\n<br>\nYou can watch his press conference here:<br>\n<br>\n<iframe allowfullscreen=\"\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"315\" src=\"/showcase/embed.aspx?title=%23Gators%20Live%20Blog%3A%20%23Swamp17%20National%20Signing%20Day&amp;youtube=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fembed%2FUOpvo3o-XwY&amp;autoplay=false\" width=\"560\"></iframe><br>\n<br>\n<br>\nIn addition, I just joined GatorVision's <dfn><a href=\"/staff.aspx?staff=474\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"474\" id=\"sidearmAd10\">Mitch Gerber</a></dfn> on Facebook Live for a breakdown of Florida's class as it currently stands. Check out FloridaGators.com later for a story off McElwain's&nbsp;press conference this afternoon.<br>\n<br>\nFor now, here is our Facebook Live --<br>\n<br>\n<iframe allowfullscreen=\"true\" allowtransparency=\"true\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"315\" scrolling=\"no\" src=\"https://www.facebook.com/plugins/video.php?href=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.facebook.com%2FGatorsFB%2Fvideos%2F1206419049405646%2F&amp;show_text=0&amp;width=560\" style=\"border:none;overflow:hidden\" width=\"560\"></iframe><br>\n<br>\n<strong>Post: 1:10 p.m.</strong><br>\n<br>\nThe Gators still expected to add to their 2017 signing class with 15 NLIs in as of this post.<br>\n<br>\nMeanwhile, with what UF has already done today, they have climbed the recruiting rankings.<br>\n<br>\nHere is a look at the latest rankings from the four major recruiting websites: <a href=\"https://n.rivals.com/team_rankings/2017\">No. 12 on Rivals.com</a>; <a href=\"http://www.scout.com/college/football/recruiting/a.z?s=73&amp;p=9&amp;c=14&amp;yr=2017\">No. 12 on Scout.com</a>; <a href=\"http://247sports.com/Season/2017-Football/CompositeTeamRankings\">No. 14 on 247Sports.com</a>; <a href=\"http://insider.espn.com/college-sports/football/recruiting/classrankings\">No. 15 on ESPN.com</a>.<br>\n<br>\nMore to come ...<br>\n<br>\n<br>\n<strong>Post: 12:45&nbsp;p.m.</strong><br>\n<br>\nThe Gators continue to stay busy on National Signing Day as cornerback C.J. Henderson and linebacker <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10344\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10344\" id=\"sidearmAd11\">Nick Smith</a></dfn> have officially signed NLIs, giving the Gators 15 signees today and counting.<br>\n<br>\nHenderson's addition set off fans on social media considering he chose the Gators over Alabama and Miami. The Hurricanes were believed to be the front-runner by many recruiting analysts but Henderson had other plans.\n<p id=\"NBMJHm\">He is ranked the No. 15 cornerback in the country and a top 25 prospect in Florida. <a href=\"https://www.periscope.tv/Comeup_5/1yNGadgZlvrKj?t=15s\">He announced his decision</a> on Periscope.tv if you want to watch.<br>\n<br>\nMeanwhile, shortly after Henderson's big announcement, Smith was welcomed to Gator Nation by head coach <dfn><a href=\"/coaches.aspx?rc=649\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"649\" id=\"sidearmAd12\">Jim McElwain</a></dfn>.<br>\n<br>\n&nbsp;</p>\n\n<twitterwidget class=\"twitter-tweet twitter-tweet-rendered\" id=\"twitter-widget-0\" style=\"position: static; visibility: visible; display: block; transform: rotate(0deg); max-width: 100%; width: 500px; min-width: 220px; margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;\" data-tweet-id=\"826845492562841613\"></twitterwidget><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet\" data-lang=\"en\" data-twitter-extracted-i1493006666309567807=\"true\">\n<p dir=\"ltr\" lang=\"en\">From Dr. Phillips High School, I'm excited to welcome <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10344\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10344\" id=\"sidearmAd13\">Nick Smith</a></dfn> to the <a href=\"https://twitter.com/GatorsFB\">@GatorsFB</a> family!! <a href=\"https://twitter.com/hashtag/Swamp17?src=hash\">#Swamp17</a> <a href=\"https://twitter.com/hashtag/GoGators?src=hash\">#GoGators</a> <a href=\"https://t.co/oPo3zi3ygW\">pic.twitter.com/oPo3zi3ygW</a></p>\n <dfn><a href=\"/coaches.aspx?rc=649\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"649\" id=\"sidearmAd14\">Jim McElwain</a></dfn> (@CoachMcElwain) <a href=\"https://twitter.com/CoachMcElwain/status/826845492562841613\">February 1, 2017</a></blockquote>\n<script async=\"\" src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><br>\nSmith is listed at 6-3, 210 pounds. He helped Orlando Dr. Phillips High reach the Class 8A state championship game and finished with four tackles and a pass breakup. A three-star prospect, those who have seen Smith in person believe he has the kind of upside that could render the ranking irrelevant during his college career.<br>\n<br>\nSmith's father, Fernando Smith, spent seven seasons in the NFL, primarily with the Minnesota Vikings in the 1990s.<br>\n<br>\n*****<br>\n<br>\n<strong>Post: 12:05 p.m.</strong><br>\n<br>\nIf you watched his commitment ceremony on Tuesday, you know 6-foot-4, 305-pound defensive lineman <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10342\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10342\" id=\"sidearmAd15\">Elijah Conliffe</a></dfn>&nbsp;has some personality.<br>\n<br>\nAnd an appetite.<br>\n&nbsp;\n<twitterwidget class=\"twitter-tweet twitter-tweet-rendered\" id=\"twitter-widget-1\" style=\"position: static; visibility: visible; display: block; transform: rotate(0deg); max-width: 100%; width: 500px; min-width: 220px; margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;\" data-tweet-id=\"826833852714872834\"></twitterwidget><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet\" data-partner=\"tweetdeck\" data-twitter-extracted-i1493006666309567807=\"true\">\n<p dir=\"ltr\" lang=\"en\">His favorite snacks are Sweet Chili Doritos and Hot Pockets. What's not to love?! ?????? <a href=\"https://t.co/h1sRcGmZut\">https://t.co/h1sRcGmZut</a></p>\n <dfn><a href=\"/staff.aspx?staff=110\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"110\" id=\"sidearmAd16\">Deidra Church</a></dfn> (@DChurchUF) <a href=\"https://twitter.com/DChurchUF/status/826833852714872834\">February 1, 2017</a></blockquote>\n<script async=\"\" src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><br>\nConliffe's NLI has officially arrived and been approved, making him the 13th official signee so far today on National Signing Day.<br>\n<br>\nLet's check out that press conference on Tuesday if you haven't seen it:<br>\n<br>\n<br>\n<br>\n<script height=\"410px\" width=\"730px\" src=\"http://player.ooyala.com/iframe.js#ec=xkdmliOTE6iZb0Yvov5DmesKArRjB8Sn&amp;pbid=55ce3a06495346ddb20768902d1e991c\"></script><iframe src=\"http://player.ooyala.com/iframe.html#ec=xkdmliOTE6iZb0Yvov5DmesKArRjB8Sn&amp;pbid=55ce3a06495346ddb20768902d1e991c&amp;docUrl=http%3A%2F%2Ffloridagators.com%2Fnews%2F2017%2F2%2F1%2Fscott-carter-gators-live-blog-swamp17-national-signing-day.aspx\" frameborder=\"0\" webkitallowfullscreen=\"true\" height=\"410px\" width=\"730px\"></iframe><br>\n<br>\n<strong>Post: 11:30 a.m.</strong><br>\n<br>\nFlorida enters the 2017 season with a talented trio at running back in <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10298\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10298\" id=\"sidearmAd17\">Jordan Scarlett</a></dfn>, <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10286\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10286\" id=\"sidearmAd18\">Lamical Perine</a></dfn> and <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10308\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10308\" id=\"sidearmAd19\">Mark Thompson</a></dfn>.<br>\n<br>\nThey have company in freshman <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10336\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10336\" id=\"sidearmAd20\">Malik Davis</a></dfn> from Jesuit High in Tampa. In talking with some Jesuit coaches during Florida's Outback Bowl practices at Jesuit, it was obvious his high school coaches saw big things for Davis in the future.<br>\n<br>\n&nbsp;\n<figure class=\"caption figure_object_image sidearm-story-image-align-left\" style=\"margin:8px; padding:2px; float:left\"><img alt=\"\" height=\"124\" src=\"http://floridagators.com/images/2017/2/1/Malik_Davis_37.jpg?width=182&amp;height=250&amp;scale=both&amp;bgcolor=003187\" style=\"display: inline-block;\" width=\"90\">\n<figcaption>Malik Davis</figcaption>\n</figure>\nSame is true for Gators running backs coach <dfn><a href=\"/coaches.aspx?rc=655\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"655\" id=\"sidearmAd21\">Tim Skipper</a></dfn>.<br>\n<br>\n\"Malik&nbsp;is a phenomenal player in space,'' Skipper said a few minutes ago. \"If you watch his tape, people cannot tackle him and he has breakaway speed.\"<br>\n<br>\nFor more from Skipper on Davis and defensive back <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10337\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10337\" id=\"sidearmAd22\">Brad Stewart</a></dfn> from New Orleans, check out the video below:<br>\n<br>\n<iframe align=\"\" allowfullscreen=\"\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"360\" src=\"/showcase/embed.aspx?Archive=5276&amp;autoplay=false\" width=\"640\"></iframe><br>\n<br>\n<br>\n<strong>Post: 10:45 a.m.</strong><br>\n<br>\nGators offensive coordinator <dfn><a href=\"/coaches.aspx?rc=652\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"652\" id=\"sidearmAd23\">Doug Nussmeier</a></dfn>&nbsp;enters his third season with another quarterback to compete in fall camp with returners <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10241\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10241\" id=\"sidearmAd24\">Luke Del Rio</a></dfn>, <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10249\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10249\" id=\"sidearmAd25\">Feleipe Franks</a></dfn> and <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10312\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10312\" id=\"sidearmAd26\">Kyle Trask</a></dfn>.<br>\n<br>\nThe Gators added St. Thomas Aquinas' <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10326\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10326\" id=\"sidearmAd27\">Jake Allen</a></dfn> officially on Wednesday, a prospect who won big in high school after competing to win the job. Allen was one of Florida's earliest commits in the 2017 class and a huge booster for the program over the past year.<br>\n<br>\n\"It's going to be another guy to come in and really create competition at the position,'' Nussmeier said. \"Jake had a phenomenal year, 13-2, won another state championship&nbsp;and first-team all-state. Really excited to add him to the mix and give us another guy that really could be the future of the quarterback position.\"<br>\n<br>\nMeanwhile, Nussmeier is also pleased Florida added a big body up front to protect those quarterbacks in offensive lineman T.J. Moore.<br>\n<br>\n\"A big, physical athletic guy,'' Nussmeier said. \"Really excited about him. Think he can come in right away and challenge to play. A real, real competitive&nbsp;kid. When you talk about the University of Florida, he understands the tradition here and the things we are trying to get accomplished.\"<br>\n<br>\nHere is more of our quick interview with Nussmeier about Allen and Moore.<br>\n<br>\n<iframe align=\"\" allowfullscreen=\"\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"360\" src=\"/showcase/embed.aspx?Archive=5275&amp;autoplay=false\" width=\"640\"></iframe><br>\n<br>\n<br>\n<strong>Post: 10:30 a.m.</strong><br>\n<br>\nHere is another video interview, this one with assistant coach Kerry Dixon, who offers his thoughts on newcomers Daquon&nbsp;Green and <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10330\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10330\" id=\"sidearmAd28\">Donovan Stiner</a></dfn>.<br>\n<br>\n<iframe align=\"\" allowfullscreen=\"\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"360\" src=\"/showcase/embed.aspx?Archive=5274&amp;autoplay=false\" width=\"640\"></iframe><br>\n<br>\n<br>\n<strong>Post: 10:20 a.m.</strong><br>\n<br>\nThe NLIs keep rolling in here inside UF's football offices.<br>\n<br>\nLinebacker Lacedrick&nbsp;Brunson out of Miami Jackson High and defensive lineman <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10341\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10341\" id=\"sidearmAd29\">Tedarrell Slaton</a></dfn> from American Heritage High are the newest Gators, giving Florida 12 official signees so far on National Signing Day. Slaton is a nice pickup for Florida and was a high school teammate of UF signees <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10328\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10328\" id=\"sidearmAd30\">Marco Wilson</a></dfn> and James Houston.<br>\n<br>\nListed at 6-4, 340, Slaton is a force on the interior line that has potential to play as a true freshman and produce.\n<p>He is the 91st-ranked player in the ESPN 300 and chose Florida over Miami and Georgia.<br>\n<br>\nMeanwhile, an interview with Gators assistant coach <dfn><a href=\"/coaches.aspx?rc=657\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"657\" id=\"sidearmAd31\">Torrian Gray</a></dfn> about defensive back signees <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10328\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10328\" id=\"sidearmAd32\">Marco Wilson</a></dfn> and <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10327\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10327\" id=\"sidearmAd33\">Shawn Davis</a></dfn>:<br>\n<br>\n<iframe align=\"\" allowfullscreen=\"\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"360\" src=\"/showcase/embed.aspx?Archive=5273&amp;autoplay=false\" width=\"640\"></iframe></p>\n<br>\n<strong>Post: 10 a.m.</strong><br>\n<br>\nWe're set up here in Florida's football offices with the GatorVision crew and grabbing quick interviews throughout the day with Gators coaches as National Signing Day unfolds. Here is the first one of the morning with head coach <dfn><a href=\"/coaches.aspx?rc=649\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"649\" id=\"sidearmAd34\">Jim McElwain</a></dfn>:<br>\n<br>\n<br>\n<strong><iframe align=\"\" allowfullscreen=\"\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"360\" src=\"/showcase/embed.aspx?Archive=5272&amp;autoplay=false\" width=\"640\"></iframe><br>\n<br>\nPost. 9:45 a.m.</strong><br>\n<br>\nThe Gators now have 10&nbsp;NLIs officially signed, sealed and delivered, the latest from linebacker <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10331\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10331\" id=\"sidearmAd35\">Ventrell Miller</a></dfn> out of Lakeland Kathleen High, defensive lineman <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10338\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10338\" id=\"sidearmAd36\">Zachary Carter</a></dfn> from Tampa Hillsborough, running back <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10336\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10336\" id=\"sidearmAd37\">Malik Davis</a></dfn> from Tampa Jesuit, defensive back <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10337\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10337\" id=\"sidearmAd38\">Brad Stewart</a></dfn> from New Orleans, and offensive lineman T.J. Moore from Mallard Creek (N.C.) High, which also produced former Gators offensive lineman D.J. Humphries.<br>\n<br>\nHad a chance to talk to assistant coach Kerry Dixon about receiver <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10329\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10329\" id=\"sidearmAd39\">Daquon Green</a></dfn>.<br>\n<br>\nDixon on Green: \"He's been loyal to us from the beginning. Was committed to us for something crazy like 19 months. When we first saw him, we just knew he was a special player with his size and strength and ability to go up and get the ball. He has a frame that we don't have.\"<br>\n<br>\n<br>\n<strong>Post 9 a.m.</strong><br>\n<br>\nThe Gators have received two more NLIs, receiver <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10329\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10329\" id=\"sidearmAd40\">Daquon Green</a></dfn> from Tampa Bay Tech and defensive back <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10330\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10330\" id=\"sidearmAd41\">Donovan Stiner</a></dfn>&nbsp;from the Houston area.<br>\n<br>\nGreen adds a potential difference maker at receiver who hauled in 41 catches for 639 yards and nine touchdowns as a senior. In four seasons at TBT, Green totaled 2,555 receiving yards and 26 touchdowns.<br>\n<br>\n&nbsp;\n<twitterwidget class=\"twitter-tweet twitter-tweet-rendered\" id=\"twitter-widget-2\" style=\"position: static; visibility: visible; display: block; transform: rotate(0deg); max-width: 100%; width: 500px; min-width: 220px; margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;\" data-tweet-id=\"825951465076318208\"></twitterwidget><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet\" data-partner=\"tweetdeck\" data-twitter-extracted-i1493006666309567807=\"true\">\n<p dir=\"ltr\" lang=\"en\"><a href=\"https://twitter.com/hashtag/Gators?src=hash\">#Gators</a> get another DB in Texas safety <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10330\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10330\" id=\"sidearmAd42\">Donovan Stiner</a></dfn> @dstinerhttp://fw.to/qFo9kRL <a href=\"https://t.co/10scT5vSoB\">pic.twitter.com/10scT5vSoB</a></p>\n Sentinel Recruiting (@OS_Recruiting) <a href=\"https://twitter.com/OS_Recruiting/status/825951465076318208\">January 30, 2017</a></blockquote>\n<script async=\"\" src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><br>\nStiner is a late pickup for the Gators to add more depth in the secondary. A 6-2, 185 physical presence out of Bellair (Texas) High, Stiner was a Houston commit until flipping to the Gators following an official visit last weekend. He had 56 tackles, one sack, three fumble recoveries and two interceptions as a senior.<br>\n<br>\nAlso, had a chance to catch up with Gators secondary coach <dfn><a href=\"/coaches.aspx?rc=657\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"657\" id=\"sidearmAd43\">Torrian Gray</a></dfn> about defensive backs <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10328\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10328\" id=\"sidearmAd44\">Marco Wilson</a></dfn> and <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10327\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10327\" id=\"sidearmAd45\">Shawn Davis</a></dfn>.<br>\n<br>\nGray on Wilson: \"Marco is an exceptional athlete. He is going to bring a lot to the table from a corner, nickel perspective.\"<br>\n<br>\nGray on Davis: \"You see a guy who can play corner, free safety, nickel. Very versatile and a natural playmaker.\"<br>\n<br>\n<br>\n<strong>Post: 8:10 a.m.</strong><br>\n<br>\nTwo more players are official -- defensive back <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10327\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10327\" id=\"sidearmAd46\">Shawn Davis</a></dfn> out of Miami Southridge High and quarterback <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10326\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10326\" id=\"sidearmAd47\">Jake Allen</a></dfn> from St. Thomas Aquinas in Fort Lauderdale.<br>\n<br>\nDavis helped Southridge win the FHSAA Class 8A state championship and finished&nbsp;with 27 tackles and two interceptions. At 5-11, 190, Davis provides another solid prospect in the secondary to join Wilson and other potential newcomers.<br>\n<br>\nMeanwhile, Allen is one of Florida's earliest commitments in the 2017 class and was a huge booster for the class. He gives Florida more depth at the quarterback position and was a two-year starter at one of the state's top prep programs.<br>\n<br>\nAllen is listed at 6-3, 200 pounds. He'll look at add weight once he arrives over the summer. Allen has winning credentials.<br>\n<br>\n&nbsp;\n<twitterwidget class=\"twitter-tweet twitter-tweet-rendered\" id=\"twitter-widget-3\" style=\"position: static; visibility: visible; display: block; transform: rotate(0deg); max-width: 100%; width: 500px; min-width: 220px; margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;\" data-tweet-id=\"826777287349719040\"></twitterwidget><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet\" data-partner=\"tweetdeck\" data-twitter-extracted-i1493006666309567807=\"true\">\n<p dir=\"ltr\" lang=\"en\">From St. Thomas Aquinas High School, I'm excited to welcome <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10326\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10326\" id=\"sidearmAd48\">Jake Allen</a></dfn> to the <a href=\"https://twitter.com/GatorsFB\">@GatorsFB</a> family! <a href=\"https://twitter.com/hashtag/Swamp17?src=hash\">#Swamp17</a> <a href=\"https://twitter.com/hashtag/GoGators?src=hash\">#GoGators</a> <a href=\"https://t.co/DlScp0ZzjF\">pic.twitter.com/DlScp0ZzjF</a></p>\n <dfn><a href=\"/coaches.aspx?rc=649\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"649\" id=\"sidearmAd49\">Jim McElwain</a></dfn> (@CoachMcElwain) <a href=\"https://twitter.com/CoachMcElwain/status/826777287349719040\">February 1, 2017</a></blockquote>\n<script async=\"\" src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><br>\nHe led Aquinas to the Class 7A Florida state title, throwing 323 yards and five touchdowns in the championship game.<br>\n<br>\nHere is a link to video of <a href=\"http://www.orlandosentinel.com/sports/florida-recruiting/blog/92098466-132.html\">Allen discussing his championship game performance</a> and decision to come to Florida.<br>\n<br>\n<br>\n<br>\n<strong>Post: 7:55 a.m.</strong><br>\n<br>\nCornerback <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10328\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10328\" id=\"sidearmAd50\">Marco Wilson</a></dfn> is officially the first player to get his NLI into Florida's compliance office this morning. Wilson is the younger brother of former Gators cornerback <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=6252\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"6252\" id=\"sidearmAd51\">Quincy Wilson</a></dfn>, who announced last month he is entering the 2017 NFL Draft.<br>\n<br>\nMarco and Quincy have a strong bond and similar skill sets. <dfn><a href=\"/roster.aspx?rp_id=10328\" rel=\"smarttag\" rev=\"10328\" id=\"sidearmAd52\">Marco Wilson</a></dfn> earned USA Today All-American honors as a senior at American Heritage, where he also ran track. Wilson is listed at 6-0, 180 pounds and picked off three passes.<br>\n<br>\nCheck this photo out. High.
